				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Der Himmel lacht! die Erde jubiliert, BWV 31 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>9 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1715 in Weimar<br />1724 in Leipzig (revised)<br />1731/35 in Leipzig (revised)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sacred_cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sacred cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Cantatas</a></span>; <h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Der Himmel lacht, die Erde jubiliert
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">The Heaven laughs! The Earth rejoices
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 31&#160;; BC A 55a-b
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 744
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>C major*
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>9 movements:
<ol><li>Sonata (C&#160;major)
</li><li>Chorus: Der Himmel lacht! Die Erde jubiliert (C&#160;major)
</li><li>Recitativo (bass): Erwünschter Tag! Sei, Seele, wieder froh! (C&#160;major-E&#160;minor)
</li><li>Aria (bass): Fürst des Lebens! starker Streiter (C&#160;major)
</li><li>Recitativo (tenor): So stehe dann, du gottergebne Seele (A&#160;minor-G&#160;major)
</li><li>Aria (tenor): Adam muß in uns verwesen (G&#160;major)
</li><li>Recitativo (soprano): Weil dann das Haupt sein Glied (E&#160;minor-C&#160;major)
</li><li>Aria (soprano): Letzte Stunde, brich herein (C&#160;major)
</li><li>Chorale: So fahr ich hin zu Jesu Christ (C&#160;major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1715 in Weimar<br />1724 in Leipzig (revised)<br />1731/35 in Leipzig (revised)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1857 (BGA)
</td></tr>
